📝 Создание (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/auto/sandbox/test-ctrlc-danger-zone.js)
```
/**
 * Test: Ctrl-C Danger Zone — Event-Driven Detection & Protection
 *
 * Проверяет:
 * 1. При Ctrl+C → main ловит "Press Ctrl-C again to exit" (ON)
 * 2. Когда Claude возвращает промпт (⏵) → danger zone снимается (OFF) — event-driven
 * 3. При /model в danger zone → команда ЖДЁТ промпта, потом выполняется
 * 4. Claude НЕ выходит
 *
 * Запуск: ./run.sh sandbox/test-ctrlc-danger-zone.js
 */

const { launch, waitForTerminal, typeCommand, waitForClaudeSessionId } = require('../core/launcher')
const electron = require('../core/electron')

const c = {
  reset: '\x1b[0m', green: '\x1b[32m', red: '\x1b[31m',
  cyan: '\x1b[36m', yellow: '\x1b[33m', dim: '\x1b[2m', bold: '\x1b[1m'
}
const log = {
  step: (m) => console.log(`${c.cyan}[STEP]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  info: (m) => console.log(`${c.dim}[INFO]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  pass: (m) => console.log(`${c.green}[PASS]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  fail: (m) => console.log(`${c.red}[FAIL]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  warn: (m) => console.log(`${c.yellow}[WARN]${c.reset} ${m}`)
}

async function sendCtrlC(page, tabId) {
  await page.evaluate((tid) => {
    const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
    ipcRenderer.send('terminal:input', tid, '\x03')
  }, tabId)
}

async function main() {
  log.step('Запуск Noted Terminal...')
  const { app, page, mainProcessLogs } = await launch({
    logConsole: false, logMainProcess: true, waitForReady: 4000
  })
  log.pass('Приложение запущено')

  try {
    log.step('Ожидание терминала...')
    await waitForTerminal(page, 15000)
    await electron.focusWindow(app)
    await page.waitForTimeout(500)

    log.step('Новый таб...')
    await page.keyboard.press('Meta+t')
    await page.waitForTimeout(1500)

    await typeCommand(page, 'cd /Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal')
    await page.waitForTimeout(2000)

    const tabId = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
      return p?.activeTabId
    })
    if (!tabId) { log.fail('Нет activeTabId'); return }
    log.info('Tab: ' + tabId)

    log.step('claude...')
    await typeCommand(page, 'claude')
    try { await waitForClaudeSessionId(page, 30000); log.pass('Session ID OK') }
    catch { log.warn('Session ID timeout') }

    log.step('Ожидание готовности (3с)...')
    await page.waitForTimeout(3000)

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════
    // TEST 1: Detection ON/OFF cycle
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════
    log.step('TEST 1: Ctrl+C → ON → prompt → OFF')
    await sendCtrlC(page, tabId)
    await page.waitForTimeout(3000)

    const onLogs = mainProcessLogs.filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone') && l.includes(': ON'))
    const offLogs = mainProcessLogs.filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone') && l.includes(': OFF'))

    const hasON = onLogs.length > 0
    const hasOFF = offLogs.length > 0
    const isEventDriven = offLogs.some(l => l.includes('event-driven'))

    if (hasON) log.pass('ON: маркер "Ctrl-C again" пойман')
    else log.fail('ON: маркер НЕ пойман')

    if (hasOFF && isEventDriven) log.pass('OFF: промпт вернулся (event-driven)')
    else if (hasOFF) log.warn('OFF: сработало, но не event-driven')
    else log.fail('OFF: danger zone не снялся')

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════
    // TEST 2: /model в danger zone
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════
    log.step('TEST 2: Ctrl+C → /model opus (в danger zone)')
    await sendCtrlC(page, tabId)
    await page.waitForTimeout(500) // дать PTY выдать маркер

    await page.evaluate((tid) => {
      const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
      ipcRenderer.send('claude:send-command', tid, '/model opus')
    }, tabId)

    await page.waitForTimeout(5000)

    const waitingLogs = mainProcessLogs.filter(l => l.includes('waiting for prompt to return'))
    const promptReturnedLogs = mainProcessLogs.filter(l => l.includes('Prompt returned, proceeding'))

    if (waitingLogs.length > 0) log.pass('WAIT: команда ждала промпта')
    else log.fail('WAIT: команда НЕ ждала')

    if (promptReturnedLogs.length > 0) log.pass('PROCEED: команда выполнена после возврата промпта')
    else log.warn('PROCEED: лог не найден')

    // Session alive?
    await page.waitForTimeout(2000)
    const state = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
      const t = p?.tabs?.get?.(p?.activeTabId)
      return { session: t?.claudeSessionId, cmd: t?.commandType }
    })
    const alive = !!(state.cmd === 'claude' || state.session)
    if (alive) log.pass('SESSION: Claude жива')
    else log.fail('SESSION: Claude вышла (' + state.cmd + ')')

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════
    // SUMMARY
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════
    console.log('\n' + c.bold + '═══════════════════════════════════════' + c.reset)
    const checks = [
      [hasON, 'Детекция ON'],
      [hasOFF && isEventDriven, 'Сброс OFF (event-driven)'],
      [waitingLogs.length > 0, 'Delay: ожидание промпта'],
      [alive, 'Сессия жива']
    ]
    checks.forEach(([ok, label]) => {
      console.log(`  [${ok ? c.green + 'PASS' : c.red + 'FAIL'}${c.reset}] ${label}`)
    })
    const allPass = checks.every(([ok]) => ok)
    console.log(allPass
      ? `\n${c.green}${c.bold}ВСЕ ТЕСТЫ ПРОЙДЕНЫ${c.reset}`
      : `\n${c.red}${c.bold}ЕСТЬ ОШИБКИ${c.reset}`)
    console.log(c.bold + '═══════════════════════════════════════' + c.reset)

    // Debug: all DangerZone logs
    console.log('\n--- DangerZone Logs ---')
    mainProcessLogs.filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone') || l.includes('send-command')).forEach(l => console.log('  ' + l.trim()))
    console.log('---')

  } finally {
    log.step('Закрытие...')
    await app.close()
  }
}

main().catch(err => { console.error(c.red + err.message + c.reset); process.exit(1) })

```

```
ON  — detected "Press Ctrl-C again to exit"

✅  Prompt returned, proceeding
    /model opus sent → Enter
```

Никаких фиксированных задержек. Danger zone снимается ровно в тот момент, когда Claude вернул промпт. Перезапусти `npm run dev` и проверь — теперь после Ctrl+C кнопка Model должна подождать промпт и сработать корректно.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user identified a bug: when pressing Ctrl+C in Claude Code CLI (which shows "Press Ctrl-C again to exit"), then immediately clicking a Model button (sonnet/opus/haiku) in the InfoPanel, Claude exits because the button's `claude:send-command` handler sends another `\x03` via `ctrlCFirst: true`. The user wanted:
   - Research how PTY output detection works in the codebase
   - Write a sandbox test in `auto/sandbox/` to verify detection of the "Press Ctrl-C again to exit" marker
   - Implement **event-driven** (not timeout-based) protection against accidental double Ctrl+C from UI buttons

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - PTY data flow: `node-pty onData()` → `parseOSC133` → Handshake → Session ID detection → `terminal:data` IPC to renderer
   - `stripVTControlCharacters()` from `node:util` for cleaning ANSI codes before text matching
   - `safePasteAndSubmit()` with `ctrlCFirst: true` sends `\x03` before pasting slash commands
   - Claude Ink TUI uses cursor motion codes (`\x1b[nC`) between words — stripped text shows `"PresCtrl-C again to exit"` (no space)
   - Event-driven Promise pattern: external `resolve` stored in Map, awaited by send-command/toggle-thinking, resolved when prompt character detected in PTY
   - Prompt detection characters: `⏵` (U+23F5), `⌵` (U+2335), `╰` (U+2570)
   - Tests require `npx electron-vite build --outDir dist` after changing `src/main/main.js` — dev server hot-reloads renderer only, not main process
   - Sending `\x03` via `page.keyboard.press('Control+c')` unreliable in Electron (intercepted as copy); must use IPC `terminal:input` directly

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **src/main/main.js** — Core changes for danger zone detection and protection:
     - Line 35: Added Map declaration:
       ```javascript
       const claudeCtrlCDangerZone = new Map(); // tabId -> { resolve, promise, timer } (event-driven clear on prompt return)
       ```
     - Lines ~856-895: Detection block in `ptyProcess.onData()`:
       ```javascript
       // ENTER danger zone
       if (sc.includes('Ctrl-C again') || sc.includes('Ctrl+C again')) {
         const prev = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
         if (prev) clearTimeout(prev.timer);
         let resolve;
         const promise = new Promise(r => { resolve = r; });
         const timer = setTimeout(() => {
           if (claudeCtrlCDangerZone.has(tabId)) {
             claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
             resolve();
           }
         }, 5000);
         claudeCtrlCDangerZone.set(tabId, { resolve, promise, timer });
         mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: true });
       }
       // EXIT danger zone: prompt returned
       const dz = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
       if (dz && (sc.includes('\u23F5') || sc.includes('\u2335') || sc.includes('\u2570'))) {
         clearTimeout(dz.timer);
         claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
         dz.resolve();
         mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: false });
       }
       ```
     - Lines ~1107-1129: `claude:send-command` handler with await:
       ```javascript
       ipcMain.on('claude:send-command', (event, tabId, command) => {
         const term = terminals.get(tabId);
         if (!term) return;
         (async () => {
           const dz = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
           if (dz) {
             console.log('[send-command] Tab ' + tabId + ': ⚠️ Danger zone active — waiting for prompt to return...');
             await dz.promise;
             console.log('[send-command] Tab ' + tabId + ': ✅ Prompt returned, proceeding');
           }
           await safePasteAndSubmit(term, command, {
             submit: true, ctrlCFirst: true,
             logPrefix: '[send-command:' + tabId + ']'
           });
         })();
       });
       ```
     - Lines ~1132-1140: `claude:toggle-thinking` handler with same await pattern:
       ```javascript
       const dz = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
       if (dz) {
         console.log('[Think] ⚠️ Danger zone active — waiting for prompt...');
         await dz.promise;
       }
       ```

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **dist/ not updated**: First test run failed because detection code was only in `src/main/main.js` but test Electron loads from `dist/`. Fix: `npx electron-vite build --outDir dist` before running tests.

```
   867→          if (prev) clearTimeout(prev.timer);
   868→
   869→          let resolve;
   870→          const promise = new Promise(r => { resolve = r; });
   871→          const timer = setTimeout(() => {
   872→            // Safety fallback: 5s max (should never be needed, prompt always returns)
   873→            if (claudeCtrlCDangerZone.has(tabId)) {
   874→              claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   875→              resolve();
   876→              console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': CLEARED (5s safety TTL)');
   877→            }
   878→          }, 5000);
   879→          claudeCtrlCDangerZone.set(tabId, { resolve, promise, timer });
   880→          console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': ON — detected "Press Ctrl-C again to exit"');
   881→          if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   882→            mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: true });
   883→          }
   884→        }
   885→
   886→        // EXIT danger zone: prompt returned (⏵ or >) while danger zone is active
   887→        const dz = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
   888→        if (dz && (sc.includes('\u23F5') || sc.includes('\u2335') || sc.includes('\u2570'))) {
   889→          // ⏵ (U+23F5) = Claude prompt, ⌵ (U+2335) = alt prompt, ╰ (U+2570) = input box bottom
   890→          clearTimeout(dz.timer);
   891→          claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   892→          dz.resolve();
   893→          console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': OFF — prompt returned (event-driven clear)');
   894→          if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   895→            mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: false });
   896→          }
   897→        }
   898→      }
   899→
```

🤖 CLAUDE:
Вот и баг. Строки 864 и 888 — обе проверки выполняются на одном и том же `sc` (одном PTY chunk). Когда Claude re-renders экран после Ctrl+C, один chunk содержит И `"Ctrl-C again"` И `⏵` (символ промпта из предыдущей строки).

Результат: DZ ставится ON (строка 879) и **мгновенно** снимается OFF (строка 891) в том же вызове `onData`. Когда `send-command` проверяет DZ — он пуст, и `safePasteAndSubmit` отправляет `\x03` напрямую → Claude выходит.

Фикс: сделать EXIT проверку через `else` — если мы только что вошли в danger zone, не проверять выход:

🤖 CLAUDE:
Готово. Суть бага:

**Проблема**: Claude Ink TUI при re-render после Ctrl+C отправляет ОДИН PTY chunk, который содержит И `"Press Ctrl-C again to exit"` И символ промпта `⏵`. Наш код ставил DZ=ON и тут же DZ=OFF в одном вызове `onData`, потому что обе проверки выполнялись последовательно на одних данных.

**Фикс**: Сделал EXIT-проверку через `else`. Если в чанке есть `"Ctrl-C again"` — ставим DZ ON и **не проверяем** символ промпта в этом же чанке. EXIT сработает только в СЛЕДУЮЩЕМ чанке PTY данных, когда Claude действительно вернёт промпт.

Перезапусти `npm run dev` и проверь — теперь даже при быстром повторном Ctrl+C + смена модели Claude не должен выходить.

📝 Создание (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/auto/sandbox/test-ctrlc-rapid-model-switch.js)
```
/**
 * Test: Rapid Model Switch + Ctrl-C cycle
 *
 * Воспроизводит баг: model switch → 1s → Ctrl+C → model switch → Claude выходит
 * Повторяет цикл 3 раза с разными моделями и логирует все DangerZone события.
 *
 * Запуск: ./run.sh sandbox/test-ctrlc-rapid-model-switch.js
 */

const { launch, waitForTerminal, typeCommand, waitForClaudeSessionId } = require('../core/launcher')
const electron = require('../core/electron')

const c = {
  reset: '\x1b[0m', green: '\x1b[32m', red: '\x1b[31m',
  cyan: '\x1b[36m', yellow: '\x1b[33m', dim: '\x1b[2m', bold: '\x1b[1m'
}
const log = {
  step: (m) => console.log(`${c.cyan}[STEP]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  info: (m) => console.log(`${c.dim}[INFO]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  pass: (m) => console.log(`${c.green}[PASS]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  fail: (m) => console.log(`${c.red}[FAIL]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  warn: (m) => console.log(`${c.yellow}[WARN]${c.reset} ${m}`)
}

async function sendCtrlC(page, tabId) {
  await page.evaluate((tid) => {
    const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
    ipcRenderer.send('terminal:input', tid, '\x03')
  }, tabId)
}

async function sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, model) {
  await page.evaluate((tid, cmd) => {
    const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
    ipcRenderer.send('claude:send-command', tid, '/model ' + cmd)
  }, tabId, model)
}

function getDZLogs(mainProcessLogs, since = 0) {
  return mainProcessLogs
    .slice(since)
    .filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone') || l.includes('send-command') || l.includes('Danger zone'))
}

async function checkSessionAlive(page) {
  const state = await page.evaluate(() => {
    const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
    const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
    const t = p?.tabs?.get?.(p?.activeTabId)
    return { session: t?.claudeSessionId, cmd: t?.commandType }
  })
  return !!(state.cmd === 'claude' || state.session)
}

async function main() {
  log.step('Запуск Noted Terminal...')
  const { app, page, mainProcessLogs } = await launch({
    logConsole: false, logMainProcess: true, waitForReady: 4000
  })
  log.pass('Приложение запущено')

  try {
    log.step('Ожидание терминала...')
    await waitForTerminal(page, 15000)
    await electron.focusWindow(app)
    await page.waitForTimeout(500)

    log.step('Новый таб...')
    await page.keyboard.press('Meta+t')
    await page.waitForTimeout(1500)

    await typeCommand(page, 'cd /Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal')
    await page.waitForTimeout(2000)

    const tabId = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
      return p?.activeTabId
    })
    if (!tabId) { log.fail('Нет activeTabId'); return }
    log.info('Tab: ' + tabId)

    log.step('claude...')
    await typeCommand(page, 'claude')
    try { await waitForClaudeSessionId(page, 30000); log.pass('Session ID OK') }
    catch { log.warn('Session ID timeout') }

    log.step('Ожидание готовности Claude (5с)...')
    await page.waitForTimeout(5000)

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // CYCLE 1: sonnet → Ctrl+C → opus (через 1с)
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const cycles = [
      { first: 'sonnet', second: 'opus', delay: 1000 },
      { first: 'sonnet', second: 'opus', delay: 500 },
      { first: 'opus', second: 'sonnet', delay: 1500 },
    ]

    const results = []

    for (let i = 0; i < cycles.length; i++) {
      const { first, second, delay } = cycles[i]
      const logStart = mainProcessLogs.length

      console.log(`\n${c.bold}═══ CYCLE ${i + 1}: /model ${first} → ${delay}ms → Ctrl+C → /model ${second} ═══${c.reset}`)

      // Step 1: Switch model (first)
      log.step(`Отправка /model ${first}...`)
      await sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, first)
      log.info(`Ожидание ${delay}ms...`)
      await page.waitForTimeout(delay)

      // Check session before Ctrl+C
      const aliveBeforeCtrlC = await checkSessionAlive(page)
      if (!aliveBeforeCtrlC) {
        log.fail(`SESSION DEAD after /model ${first} (before Ctrl+C)`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: 'died after first model switch' })
        break
      }
      log.pass(`Session alive after /model ${first}`)

      // Step 2: Ctrl+C
      log.step('Ctrl+C...')
      await sendCtrlC(page, tabId)
      await page.waitForTimeout(500) // дать PTY выдать маркер

      // Step 3: Immediately switch model again
      log.step(`Отправка /model ${second} (в potential danger zone)...`)
      await sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, second)

      // Step 4: Wait for everything to settle
      log.info('Ожидание обработки (6с)...')
      await page.waitForTimeout(6000)

      // Step 5: Check session alive
      const alive = await checkSessionAlive(page)

      // Step 6: Dump DZ logs for this cycle
      const dzLogs = getDZLogs(mainProcessLogs, logStart)
      console.log(`\n--- DZ Logs (Cycle ${i + 1}) ---`)
      dzLogs.forEach(l => console.log('  ' + l.trim()))
      console.log('---')

      const hasON = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes(': ON'))
      const hasOFF = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes(': OFF'))
      const hasWait = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes('waiting for prompt'))
      const hasProceed = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes('Prompt returned'))

      log.info(`DZ ON: ${hasON}, OFF: ${hasOFF}, Wait: ${hasWait}, Proceed: ${hasProceed}`)

      if (alive) {
        log.pass(`Cycle ${i + 1}: SESSION ALIVE`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: true })
      } else {
        log.fail(`Cycle ${i + 1}: SESSION DEAD — Claude вышла!`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: 'Claude exited' })
        break // no point continuing
      }
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // SUMMARY
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    console.log(`\n${c.bold}═══════════════════════════════════════${c.reset}`)
    console.log(`${c.bold}SUMMARY${c.reset}`)
    results.forEach(r => {
      const icon = r.pass ? `${c.green}PASS` : `${c.red}FAIL`
      console.log(`  [${icon}${c.reset}] Cycle ${r.cycle}${r.reason ? ' — ' + r.reason : ''}`)
    })
    const allPass = results.length === cycles.length && results.every(r => r.pass)
    console.log(allPass
      ? `\n${c.green}${c.bold}ВСЕ ЦИКЛЫ ПРОЙДЕНЫ${c.reset}`
      : `\n${c.red}${c.bold}ЕСТЬ ОШИБКИ${c.reset}`)
    console.log(`${c.bold}═══════════════════════════════════════${c.reset}`)

    // Full DZ log dump
    console.log('\n--- ALL DangerZone + send-command Logs ---')
    mainProcessLogs
      .filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone') || l.includes('send-command') || l.includes('Danger zone'))
      .forEach(l => console.log('  ' + l.trim()))
    console.log('---')

  } finally {
    log.step('Закрытие...')
    await app.close()
  }
}

main().catch(err => { console.error(c.red + err.message + c.reset); process.exit(1) })

```

**Actions:**
📄 Чтение (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/src/main/main.js)
```
   855→
   856→      // ========== CTRL-C DANGER ZONE DETECTION ==========
   857→      // Claude shows "Press Ctrl-C again to exit" after first Ctrl+C.
   858→      // If we send another Ctrl+C (e.g. from send-command ctrlCFirst), Claude exits.
   859→      // Event-driven: ON when marker detected, OFF when prompt (⏵ or >) returns.
   860→      {
   861→        const sc = stripVTControlCharacters(data);
   862→
   863→        // ENTER danger zone: detected "Ctrl-C again" in PTY output
   864→        if (sc.includes('Ctrl-C again') || sc.includes('Ctrl+C again')) {
   865→          // Clean up previous if any
   866→          const prev = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
   867→          if (prev) clearTimeout(prev.timer);
   868→
   869→          let resolve;
   870→          const promise = new Promise(r => { resolve = r; });
   871→          const timer = setTimeout(() => {
   872→            // Safety fallback: 5s max (should never be needed, prompt always returns)
   873→            if (claudeCtrlCDangerZone.has(tabId)) {
   874→              claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   875→              resolve();
   876→              console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': CLEARED (5s safety TTL)');
   877→            }
   878→          }, 5000);
   879→          claudeCtrlCDangerZone.set(tabId, { resolve, promise, timer });
   880→          console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': ON — detected "Press Ctrl-C again to exit"');
   881→          if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   882→            mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: true });
   883→          }
   884→        } else {
   885→          // EXIT danger zone: prompt returned (⏵ or >) while danger zone is active
   886→          // CRITICAL: must be `else` — Claude Ink TUI re-renders full screen after Ctrl+C,
   887→          // so a single PTY chunk can contain BOTH "Ctrl-C again" AND ⏵ prompt char.
   888→          // Without `else`, DZ would be set ON and immediately cleared OFF in same onData call.
   889→          const dz = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
   890→          if (dz && (sc.includes('\u23F5') || sc.includes('\u2335') || sc.includes('\u2570'))) {
   891→            // ⏵ (U+23F5) = Claude prompt, ⌵ (U+2335) = alt prompt, ╰ (U+2570) = input box bottom
   892→            clearTimeout(dz.timer);
   893→            claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   894→            dz.resolve();
   895→            console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': OFF — prompt returned (event-driven clear)');
   896→            if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   897→              mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: false });
   898→            }
   899→          }
   900→        }
   901→      }
   902→
   903→      // Send raw data to renderer - xterm.js handles OSC sequences itself
   904→      if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
```

```
/**
 * Test: Rapid Model Switch + Ctrl-C cycle
 *
 * Воспроизводит баг: model switch → 1s → Ctrl+C → model switch → Claude выходит
 * С активным мониторингом сессии Claude после каждого шага.
 *
 * Запуск: ./run.sh sandbox/test-ctrlc-rapid-model-switch.js
 */

const { launch, waitForTerminal, typeCommand, waitForClaudeSessionId } = require('../core/launcher')
const electron = require('../core/electron')

const c = {
  reset: '\x1b[0m', green: '\x1b[32m', red: '\x1b[31m',
  cyan: '\x1b[36m', yellow: '\x1b[33m', dim: '\x1b[2m', bold: '\x1b[1m'
}
const log = {
  step: (m) => console.log(`${c.cyan}[STEP]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  info: (m) => console.log(`${c.dim}[INFO]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  pass: (m) => console.log(`${c.green}[PASS]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  fail: (m) => console.log(`${c.red}[FAIL]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  warn: (m) => console.log(`${c.yellow}[WARN]${c.reset} ${m}`)
}

async function sendCtrlC(page, tabId) {
  await page.evaluate((tid) => {
    const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
    ipcRenderer.send('terminal:input', tid, '\x03')
  }, tabId)
}

async function sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, model) {
  await page.evaluate(({ tid, cmd }) => {
    const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
    ipcRenderer.send('claude:send-command', tid, '/model ' + cmd)
  }, { tid: tabId, cmd: model })
}

async function getSessionState(page) {
  return await page.evaluate(() => {
    const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
    const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
    const t = p?.tabs?.get?.(p?.activeTabId)
    return {
      session: t?.claudeSessionId,
      cmd: t?.commandType,
      tabId: t?.id,
      tabName: t?.name
    }
  })
}

async function isClaudeAlive(page) {
  const state = await getSessionState(page)
  return { alive: !!(state.cmd === 'claude' || state.session), state }
}

function getDZLogs(mainProcessLogs, since = 0) {
  return mainProcessLogs
    .slice(since)
    .filter(l =>
      l.includes('DangerZone') ||
      l.includes('DZ-DIAG') ||
      l.includes('send-command') ||
      l.includes('Danger zone')
    )
}

async function main() {
  log.step('Запуск Noted Terminal...')
  const { app, page, mainProcessLogs } = await launch({
    logConsole: false, logMainProcess: true, waitForReady: 4000
  })
  log.pass('Приложение запущено')

  try {
    log.step('Ожидание терминала...')
    await waitForTerminal(page, 15000)
    await electron.focusWindow(app)
    await page.waitForTimeout(500)

    log.step('Новый таб...')
    await page.keyboard.press('Meta+t')
    await page.waitForTimeout(1500)

    await typeCommand(page, 'cd /Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal')
    await page.waitForTimeout(2000)

    const tabId = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
      return p?.activeTabId
    })
    if (!tabId) { log.fail('Нет activeTabId'); return }
    log.info('Tab: ' + tabId)

    log.step('claude...')
    await typeCommand(page, 'claude')
    try { await waitForClaudeSessionId(page, 30000); log.pass('Session ID OK') }
    catch { log.warn('Session ID timeout') }

    // Check initial session state
    const initState = await isClaudeAlive(page)
    log.info('Initial state: ' + JSON.stringify(initState.state))
    if (!initState.alive) { log.fail('Claude не запустилась!'); return }

    log.step('Ожидание готовности Claude (5с)...')
    await page.waitForTimeout(5000)

    // Re-check after wait
    const preState = await isClaudeAlive(page)
    log.info('Pre-test state: cmd=' + preState.state.cmd + ', session=' + (preState.state.session ? 'YES' : 'NO'))
    if (!preState.alive) { log.fail('Claude умерла до начала тестов!'); return }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // CYCLES: model switch → delay → Ctrl+C → model switch
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const cycles = [
      { first: 'sonnet', second: 'opus', delay: 1500 },
      { first: 'sonnet', second: 'opus', delay: 1000 },
      { first: 'opus', second: 'sonnet', delay: 500 },
    ]

    const results = []

    for (let i = 0; i < cycles.length; i++) {
      const { first, second, delay } = cycles[i]
      const logStart = mainProcessLogs.length

      console.log(`\n${c.bold}═══ CYCLE ${i + 1}: /model ${first} → ${delay}ms → Ctrl+C → /model ${second} ═══${c.reset}`)

      // CHECK: session alive before anything
      const beforeSwitch = await isClaudeAlive(page)
      if (!beforeSwitch.alive) {
        log.fail(`DEAD BEFORE CYCLE ${i + 1} — cmd=${beforeSwitch.state.cmd}`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: 'dead before start' })
        break
      }

      // Step 1: Switch model (first)
      log.step(`[1/4] Отправка /model ${first}...`)
      await sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, first)

      // Wait for model switch to complete
      log.info(`Ожидание завершения model switch (4с)...`)
      await page.waitForTimeout(4000)

      // CHECK: session alive after model switch
      const afterSwitch = await isClaudeAlive(page)
      if (!afterSwitch.alive) {
        log.fail(`DEAD after /model ${first} — cmd=${afterSwitch.state.cmd}`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: `died after /model ${first}` })
        break
      }
      log.pass(`Session alive after /model ${first}`)

      // Step 2: Wait the specified delay
      log.info(`Ожидание ${delay}ms перед Ctrl+C...`)
      await page.waitForTimeout(delay)

      // Step 3: Ctrl+C
      log.step('[2/4] Ctrl+C...')
      await sendCtrlC(page, tabId)

      // Wait for "Press Ctrl-C again" to appear in PTY
      log.info('Ожидание маркера danger zone (2с)...')
      await page.waitForTimeout(2000)

      // CHECK: session alive after Ctrl+C
      const afterCtrlC = await isClaudeAlive(page)
      if (!afterCtrlC.alive) {
        log.fail(`DEAD after Ctrl+C — cmd=${afterCtrlC.state.cmd}`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: 'died after Ctrl+C' })
        break
      }
      log.pass('Session alive after Ctrl+C')

      // Check if DZ was set
      const dzOnLogs = mainProcessLogs.slice(logStart).filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone') && l.includes(': ON'))
      if (dzOnLogs.length > 0) {
        log.pass('DZ ON detected')
      } else {
        log.warn('DZ ON NOT detected after Ctrl+C!')
      }

      // Step 4: Switch model (second) — this is the dangerous moment
      log.step(`[3/4] Отправка /model ${second} (в danger zone)...`)
      await sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, second)

      // Wait for everything to settle
      log.info('Ожидание обработки (6с)...')
      await page.waitForTimeout(6000)

      // Step 5: CHECK session alive after second model switch
      const afterSecondSwitch = await isClaudeAlive(page)

      // Dump DZ logs for this cycle
      const dzLogs = getDZLogs(mainProcessLogs, logStart)
      console.log(`\n--- DZ/DIAG Logs (Cycle ${i + 1}) ---`)
      dzLogs.forEach(l => console.log('  ' + l.trim()))
      console.log('---')

      const hasON = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes('DangerZone') && l.includes(': ON'))
      const hasOFF = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes('DangerZone') && l.includes(': OFF'))
      const hasWait = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes('waiting for prompt'))
      const diagChunks = dzLogs.filter(l => l.includes('DZ-DIAG'))

      log.info(`DZ ON: ${hasON}, OFF: ${hasOFF}, Wait: ${hasWait}, DIAG chunks: ${diagChunks.length}`)

      if (afterSecondSwitch.alive) {
        log.pass(`Cycle ${i + 1}: SESSION ALIVE after /model ${second}`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: true })
      } else {
        log.fail(`Cycle ${i + 1}: SESSION DEAD — Claude вышла! cmd=${afterSecondSwitch.state.cmd}`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: `Claude exited after /model ${second}` })
        break
      }
    }

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // SUMMARY
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    console.log(`\n${c.bold}═══════════════════════════════════════${c.reset}`)
    console.log(`${c.bold}SUMMARY${c.reset}`)
    results.forEach(r => {
      const icon = r.pass ? `${c.green}PASS` : `${c.red}FAIL`
      console.log(`  [${icon}${c.reset}] Cycle ${r.cycle}${r.reason ? ' — ' + r.reason : ''}`)
    })
    const allPass = results.length === cycles.length && results.every(r => r.pass)
    console.log(allPass
      ? `\n${c.green}${c.bold}ВСЕ ЦИКЛЫ ПРОЙДЕНЫ${c.reset}`
      : `\n${c.red}${c.bold}ЕСТЬ ОШИБКИ${c.reset}`)
    console.log(`${c.bold}═══════════════════════════════════════${c.reset}`)

    // Full DZ/DIAG log dump
    console.log('\n--- ALL DangerZone + DZ-DIAG + send-command Logs ---')
    mainProcessLogs
      .filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone') || l.includes('DZ-DIAG') || l.includes('send-command') || l.includes('Danger zone'))
      .forEach(l => console.log('  ' + l.trim()))
    console.log('---')

  } finally {
    log.step('Закрытие...')
    await app.close()
  }
}

main().catch(err => { console.error(c.red + err.message + c.reset); process.exit(1) })

```

```
✓ built in 3.16s
```

🤖 CLAUDE:
<thinking>
Interesting! Now all 3 cycles pass AND the DZ detection works properly:
- Cycle 1: DZ ON → OFF (event-driven). Session alive.
- Cycle 2: DZ ON → OFF (event-driven). Session alive.
- Cycle 3: DZ ON → OFF (event-driven). Session alive.

The `else` fix is working! But wait - the user says it still doesn't work in their actual app. 

Key observations from the DIAG logs:
1. The stripped text shows `"PresCtrl-C again to exit"` (no space after "Pres") — this is because Claude's Ink TUI uses cursor moti...[truncated]
</thinking>

🤖 CLAUDE:
Все тесты PASS и DZ работает. Но ключевое наблюдение из DIAG:

```
DZ ON → DZ OFF (prompt returned) — happens in milliseconds!
```

Вот проблема: после Ctrl+C Claude re-renders весь экран. **Первый chunk** содержит "Ctrl-C again" (DZ ON). **Второй chunk через пару ms** содержит `⏵` от предыдущего prompt (DZ OFF). DZ живёт миллисекунды, а Claude's warning активен **3-4 секунды**.

Наш `send-command` проверяет DZ, но оно уже снято. Он шлёт `\x03` через ctrlCFirst → Claude exit.

Нужен **minimum hold** — не очищать DZ раньше чем через 3 секунды (столько длится warning в Claude).

🤖 CLAUDE:

**Actions:**
📄 Чтение (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/src/main/main.js)
```
   856→      // ========== CTRL-C DANGER ZONE DETECTION ==========
   857→      // Claude shows "Press Ctrl-C again to exit" after first Ctrl+C.
   858→      // If we send another Ctrl+C (e.g. from send-command ctrlCFirst), Claude exits.
   859→      // Event-driven: ON when marker detected, OFF when prompt (⏵ or >) returns.
   860→      {
   861→        const sc = stripVTControlCharacters(data);
   862→
   863→        // DIAG: log chunks containing ctrl-c or exit-related text
   864→        const scLower = sc.toLowerCase();
   865→        if (scLower.includes('ctrl') || scLower.includes('again') || scLower.includes('exit')) {
   866→          const preview = sc.replace(/\n/g, '\\n').substring(0, 200);
   867→          console.log('[DZ-DIAG] Tab ' + tabId + ': chunk=' + data.length + 'B stripped="' + preview + '"');
   868→        }
   869→
   870→        // ENTER danger zone: detected "Ctrl-C again" in PTY output
   871→        if (sc.includes('Ctrl-C again') || sc.includes('Ctrl+C again')) {
   872→          // Clean up previous if any
   873→          const prev = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
   874→          if (prev) clearTimeout(prev.timer);
   875→
   876→          let resolve;
   877→          const promise = new Promise(r => { resolve = r; });
   878→          const timer = setTimeout(() => {
   879→            // Safety fallback: 5s max (should never be needed, prompt always returns)
   880→            if (claudeCtrlCDangerZone.has(tabId)) {
   881→              claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   882→              resolve();
   883→              console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': CLEARED (5s safety TTL)');
   884→            }
   885→          }, 5000);
   886→          claudeCtrlCDangerZone.set(tabId, { resolve, promise, timer });
   887→          console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': ON — detected "Press Ctrl-C again to exit"');
   888→          if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   889→            mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: true });
   890→          }
   891→        } else {
   892→          // EXIT danger zone: prompt returned (⏵ or >) while danger zone is active
   893→          // CRITICAL: must be `else` — Claude Ink TUI re-renders full screen after Ctrl+C,
   894→          // so a single PTY chunk can contain BOTH "Ctrl-C again" AND ⏵ prompt char.
   895→          // Without `else`, DZ would be set ON and immediately cleared OFF in same onData call.
   896→          const dz = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
   897→          if (dz && (sc.includes('\u23F5') || sc.includes('\u2335') || sc.includes('\u2570'))) {
   898→            // ⏵ (U+23F5) = Claude prompt, ⌵ (U+2335) = alt prompt, ╰ (U+2570) = input box bottom
   899→            clearTimeout(dz.timer);
   900→            claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   901→            dz.resolve();
   902→            console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': OFF — prompt returned (event-driven clear)');
   903→            if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   904→              mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: false });
   905→            }
   906→          }
   907→        }
   908→      }
   909→
   910→      // Send raw data to renderer - xterm.js handles OSC sequences itself
```

**Actions:**
📝 Создание (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/auto/sandbox/test-ctrlc-rapid-model-switch.js)
```
/**
 * Test: Rapid Model Switch + Ctrl-C cycle
 *
 * Воспроизводит баг: model switch → short delay → Ctrl+C → model switch → Claude exits
 * Verifies that DZ holds for 3+ seconds and send-command waits.
 *
 * Запуск: ./run.sh sandbox/test-ctrlc-rapid-model-switch.js
 */

const { launch, waitForTerminal, typeCommand, waitForClaudeSessionId } = require('../core/launcher')
const electron = require('../core/electron')

const c = {
  reset: '\x1b[0m', green: '\x1b[32m', red: '\x1b[31m',
  cyan: '\x1b[36m', yellow: '\x1b[33m', dim: '\x1b[2m', bold: '\x1b[1m'
}
const log = {
  step: (m) => console.log(`${c.cyan}[STEP]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  info: (m) => console.log(`${c.dim}[INFO]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  pass: (m) => console.log(`${c.green}[PASS]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  fail: (m) => console.log(`${c.red}[FAIL]${c.reset} ${m}`),
  warn: (m) => console.log(`${c.yellow}[WARN]${c.reset} ${m}`)
}

async function sendCtrlC(page, tabId) {
  await page.evaluate((tid) => {
    const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
    ipcRenderer.send('terminal:input', tid, '\x03')
  }, tabId)
}

async function sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, model) {
  await page.evaluate(({ tid, cmd }) => {
    const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron')
    ipcRenderer.send('claude:send-command', tid, '/model ' + cmd)
  }, { tid: tabId, cmd: model })
}

async function isClaudeAlive(page) {
  const state = await page.evaluate(() => {
    const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
    const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
    const t = p?.tabs?.get?.(p?.activeTabId)
    return { session: t?.claudeSessionId, cmd: t?.commandType }
  })
  return { alive: !!(state.cmd === 'claude' || state.session), state }
}

async function main() {
  log.step('Запуск Noted Terminal...')
  const { app, page, mainProcessLogs } = await launch({
    logConsole: false, logMainProcess: true, waitForReady: 4000
  })
  log.pass('Приложение запущено')

  try {
    log.step('Ожидание терминала...')
    await waitForTerminal(page, 15000)
    await electron.focusWindow(app)
    await page.waitForTimeout(500)

    log.step('Новый таб...')
    await page.keyboard.press('Meta+t')
    await page.waitForTimeout(1500)

    await typeCommand(page, 'cd /Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal')
    await page.waitForTimeout(2000)

    const tabId = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const s = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      const p = s?.openProjects?.get?.(s?.activeProjectId)
      return p?.activeTabId
    })
    if (!tabId) { log.fail('Нет activeTabId'); return }
    log.info('Tab: ' + tabId)

    log.step('claude...')
    await typeCommand(page, 'claude')
    try { await waitForClaudeSessionId(page, 30000); log.pass('Session ID OK') }
    catch { log.warn('Session ID timeout') }

    log.step('Ожидание готовности Claude (5с)...')
    await page.waitForTimeout(5000)

    const preState = await isClaudeAlive(page)
    if (!preState.alive) { log.fail('Claude не запустилась!'); return }
    log.pass('Claude alive, начинаем тесты')

    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    // CYCLE 1: /model sonnet → 1.5s → Ctrl+C → immediately /model opus
    // This is the exact user scenario: switch model, quickly Ctrl+C, switch again
    // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    const cycles = [
      { first: 'sonnet', second: 'opus',   delayBeforeCtrlC: 1500, delayBeforeSecondSwitch: 300 },
      { first: 'opus',   second: 'sonnet', delayBeforeCtrlC: 1000, delayBeforeSecondSwitch: 500 },
      { first: 'sonnet', second: 'opus',   delayBeforeCtrlC: 500,  delayBeforeSecondSwitch: 200 },
    ]

    const results = []

    for (let i = 0; i < cycles.length; i++) {
      const { first, second, delayBeforeCtrlC, delayBeforeSecondSwitch } = cycles[i]
      const logStart = mainProcessLogs.length

      console.log(`\n${c.bold}═══ CYCLE ${i + 1}: /model ${first} → ${delayBeforeCtrlC}ms → Ctrl+C → ${delayBeforeSecondSwitch}ms → /model ${second} ═══${c.reset}`)

      // Check alive before
      const before = await isClaudeAlive(page)
      if (!before.alive) {
        log.fail(`DEAD BEFORE CYCLE ${i + 1}`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: 'dead before start' })
        break
      }

      // Step 1: Model switch
      log.step(`[1] /model ${first}`)
      await sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, first)

      // Wait for model switch to complete (need enough time for safePasteAndSubmit + model output)
      await page.waitForTimeout(5000)

      const afterFirst = await isClaudeAlive(page)
      if (!afterFirst.alive) {
        log.fail(`DEAD after /model ${first}`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: `died after /model ${first}` })
        break
      }
      log.pass(`Alive after /model ${first}`)

      // Step 2: Wait, then Ctrl+C
      log.info(`Wait ${delayBeforeCtrlC}ms...`)
      await page.waitForTimeout(delayBeforeCtrlC)

      log.step('[2] Ctrl+C')
      await sendCtrlC(page, tabId)

      // Step 3: Short delay, then second model switch (the dangerous part)
      log.info(`Wait ${delayBeforeSecondSwitch}ms...`)
      await page.waitForTimeout(delayBeforeSecondSwitch)

      const afterCtrlC = await isClaudeAlive(page)
      if (!afterCtrlC.alive) {
        log.fail('DEAD after Ctrl+C')
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: 'died after Ctrl+C' })
        break
      }

      log.step(`[3] /model ${second} (DANGER: should be protected by DZ hold)`)
      await sendModelSwitch(page, tabId, second)

      // Wait for DZ to expire + model switch to complete
      // DZ hold = 3s, TTL = 4s, plus safePasteAndSubmit time
      log.info('Wait 8s for DZ + model switch...')
      await page.waitForTimeout(8000)

      // Final check
      const afterSecond = await isClaudeAlive(page)

      // Collect DZ logs
      const cycleLogs = mainProcessLogs.slice(logStart)
      const dzLogs = cycleLogs.filter(l =>
        l.includes('DangerZone') || l.includes('send-command') && (l.includes('waiting') || l.includes('Prompt returned'))
      )

      console.log(`\n--- Key Logs (Cycle ${i + 1}) ---`)
      cycleLogs.filter(l =>
        l.includes('DangerZone') || l.includes('DZ-DIAG') ||
        (l.includes('send-command') && !l.includes('Start:'))
      ).forEach(l => console.log('  ' + l.trim()))
      console.log('---')

      const hasON = dzLogs.some(l => l.includes(': ON'))
      const hasWait = cycleLogs.some(l => l.includes('waiting for prompt'))
      const hasTTL = cycleLogs.some(l => l.includes('TTL expired'))

      log.info(`DZ ON: ${hasON}, Wait: ${hasWait}, TTL: ${hasTTL}`)

      if (afterSecond.alive) {
        log.pass(`CYCLE ${i + 1}: SESSION ALIVE`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: true })
      } else {
        log.fail(`CYCLE ${i + 1}: SESSION DEAD`)
        results.push({ cycle: i + 1, pass: false, reason: `died after /model ${second}` })
        break
      }
    }

    // SUMMARY
    console.log(`\n${c.bold}═══════════════════════════════════════${c.reset}`)
    results.forEach(r => {
      const icon = r.pass ? `${c.green}PASS` : `${c.red}FAIL`
      console.log(`  [${icon}${c.reset}] Cycle ${r.cycle}${r.reason ? ' — ' + r.reason : ''}`)
    })
    const allPass = results.length === cycles.length && results.every(r => r.pass)
    console.log(allPass
      ? `\n${c.green}${c.bold}ВСЕ ЦИКЛЫ ПРОЙДЕНЫ${c.reset}`
      : `\n${c.red}${c.bold}ЕСТЬ ОШИБКИ${c.reset}`)
    console.log(`${c.bold}═══════════════════════════════════════${c.reset}`)

    // All DZ logs
    console.log('\n--- ALL DZ Logs ---')
    mainProcessLogs
      .filter(l => l.includes('DangerZone'))
      .forEach(l => console.log('  ' + l.trim()))
    console.log('---')

  } finally {
    log.step('Закрытие...')
    await app.close()
  }
}

main().catch(err => { console.error(c.red + err.message + c.reset); process.exit(1) })

```

<thinking>
Interesting! All 3 cycles pass but:

- Cycle 1: DZ ON from model switch's ctrlCFirst → TTL expired (4s) → cleared. No DZ from user Ctrl+C, no "waiting" log.
- Cycle 2: NO DZ ON at all! Neither from model switch nor from user Ctrl+C.
- Cycle 3: NO DZ ON at all!

So the DZ detection still only fires in Cycle 1 for the model switch's own ctrlCFirst, and never fires for the user's Ctrl+C (steps 2-3 in each cycle). This is the core problem — the user's Ctrl+C doesn't trigger DZ detection.

🤖 CLAUDE:
Ключевое открытие! В Cycles 2 и 3 DZ ON не срабатывает для **пользовательского** Ctrl+C. Из предыдущего DIAG видно разницу:

- ctrlCFirst `\x03`: `"PresCtrl-C again to exit"` → содержит `"Ctrl-C again"` ✅
- User Ctrl+C: `"Press Ctrl-Cagain to exit"` → содержит `"Ctrl-Cagain"` (без пробела) ❌

Claude Ink TUI по-разному форматирует курсор для разных источников `\x03`! Наш паттерн `sc.includes('Ctrl-C again')` не ловит user Ctrl+C.

Фикс: использовать более стабильный паттерн `"again to exit"`:

🤖 CLAUDE:
**Все 3 цикла PASS!** И теперь видно как система работает правильно:

```
Cycle 1 (300ms delay):
  [2] Ctrl+C
  DZ ON ← user Ctrl+C ловится!
  [3] /model opus
  ⚠️ Danger zone active — waiting for prompt to return...  ← ЖДЁТ!
  DZ CLEARED (TTL expired)  ← 4с прошло
  ✅ Prompt returned, proceeding  ← теперь безопасно
  SESSION ALIVE ✅

Cycle 2 (500ms delay): Same pattern — Wait: true ✅
Cycle 3 (200ms delay): Same pattern — Wait: true ✅
```

Все 3 ключевых fix'а работают вместе:
1. **`else`** — не снимать DZ в том же PTY chunk
2. **`"again to exit"`** — ловит оба формата stripped text
3. **Min hold 3s + TTL 4s** — DZ держится пока Claude's warning активен

📄 Чтение (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/src/main/main.js)
```
   856→      // ========== CTRL-C DANGER ZONE DETECTION ==========
   857→      // Claude shows "Press Ctrl-C again to exit" after first Ctrl+C.
   858→      // If we send another Ctrl+C (e.g. from send-command ctrlCFirst), Claude exits.
   859→      // Hybrid: ON when marker detected, OFF when prompt returns AFTER minimum hold (3s).
   860→      // Why min hold: Claude's Ink TUI re-renders full screen immediately after Ctrl+C,
   861→      // and that re-render includes ⏵ prompt char. Without min hold, DZ would be set ON
   862→      // and cleared OFF within milliseconds — but Claude's warning lasts ~3-4 seconds.
   863→      {
   864→        const sc = stripVTControlCharacters(data);
   865→
   866→        // ENTER danger zone: detected "Press Ctrl-C again to exit" in PTY output
   867→        // Claude Ink TUI uses cursor motion codes — after stripping, text can be:
   868→        //   "PresCtrl-C again to exit" (from ctrlCFirst \x03)
   869→        //   "Press Ctrl-Cagain to exit" (from user keyboard \x03)
   870→        // Match "again to exit" which is stable across all variants.
   871→        if (sc.includes('again to exit')) {
   872→          // Clean up previous if any
   873→          const prev = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
   874→          if (prev) clearTimeout(prev.timer);
   875→
   876→          let resolve;
   877→          const promise = new Promise(r => { resolve = r; });
   878→          const timer = setTimeout(() => {
   879→            // Safety fallback: clear after Claude's warning expires (~4s)
   880→            if (claudeCtrlCDangerZone.has(tabId)) {
   881→              claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   882→              resolve();
   883→              console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': CLEARED (TTL expired)');
   884→              if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   885→                mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: false });
   886→              }
   887→            }
   888→          }, 4000);
   889→          claudeCtrlCDangerZone.set(tabId, { resolve, promise, timer, setAt: Date.now() });
   890→          console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': ON — detected "Press Ctrl-C again to exit"');
   891→          if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   892→            mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: true });
   893→          }
   894→        } else {
   895→          // EXIT danger zone: prompt returned (⏵ or >) while danger zone is active
   896→          // CRITICAL: must be `else` — same PTY chunk can contain both marker and ⏵.
   897→          // CRITICAL: minimum hold 3s — Claude re-renders ⏵ immediately after Ctrl-C
   898→          // but warning lasts ~3-4 seconds. Only accept ⏵ after min hold.
   899→          const dz = claudeCtrlCDangerZone.get(tabId);
   900→          if (dz && (Date.now() - dz.setAt >= 3000) &&
   901→              (sc.includes('\u23F5') || sc.includes('\u2335') || sc.includes('\u2570'))) {
   902→            // ⏵ (U+23F5) = Claude prompt, ⌵ (U+2335) = alt prompt, ╰ (U+2570) = input box bottom
   903→            clearTimeout(dz.timer);
   904→            claudeCtrlCDangerZone.delete(tabId);
   905→            dz.resolve();
   906→            console.log('[CtrlC-DangerZone] Tab ' + tabId + ': OFF — prompt returned after hold (event-driven)');
   907→            if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
   908→              mainWindow.webContents.send('claude:ctrlc-danger-zone', { tabId, active: false });
   909→            }
   910→          }
   911→        }
   912→      }
   913→
   914→      // Send raw data to renderer - xterm.js handles OSC sequences itself
   915→      if (mainWindow && !mainWindow.isDestroyed()) {
```

| # | Баг | Фикс |
|---|-----|------|

Проверю, что toggle-thinking делает на самом деле:

🤖 CLAUDE:

**Actions:**
📄 Чтение (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/src/main/main.js)
```
  1185→  const stripped = require('node:util').stripVTControlCharacters;
  1186→
  1187→  return new Promise((resolve) => {
  1188→    let buffer = '';
  1189→
  1190→    const sub = term.onData((data) => {
  1191→      buffer += data;
  1192→
  1193→      // Picker ready when synchronized output ends
  1194→      if (!buffer.includes('\x1b[?2026l')) return;
  1195→      sub.dispose();
  1196→
  1197→      const clean = stripped(buffer);
  1198→      const enabledIdx = clean.indexOf('Enabled');
  1199→      const disabledIdx = clean.indexOf('Disabled');
  1200→      const checkIdx = clean.indexOf('\u2714'); // ✓
  1201→
  1202→      let wasEnabled = true;
  1203→      if (checkIdx >= 0 && enabledIdx >= 0 && disabledIdx >= 0) {
  1204→        wasEnabled = Math.abs(checkIdx - enabledIdx) < Math.abs(checkIdx - disabledIdx);
  1205→      }
  1206→
  1207→      const newState = !wasEnabled;
  1208→      console.log('[Think] clean text:', JSON.stringify(clean).substring(0, 400));
  1209→      console.log('[Think] enabledIdx:', enabledIdx, 'disabledIdx:', disabledIdx, 'checkIdx:', checkIdx);
  1210→      console.log('[Think] Was:', wasEnabled ? 'Enabled' : 'Disabled', '-> Toggling to:', newState ? 'Enabled' : 'Disabled');
  1211→
  1212→      // Navigate to the other option
  1213→      const arrow = wasEnabled ? '\x1b[B' : '\x1b[A';
  1214→      console.log('[Think] Sending arrow:', wasEnabled ? 'DOWN' : 'UP');
  1215→      term.write(arrow);
  1216→
  1217→      // Confirm with Enter after Ink processes the arrow
  1218→      let confirmResolved = false;
  1219→      const confirmSub = term.onData((confirmData) => {
  1220→        if (confirmResolved) return;
  1221→        console.log('[Think] Arrow response RAW (' + confirmData.length + ' bytes):', JSON.stringify(confirmData).substring(0, 300));
  1222→        confirmSub.dispose();
  1223→        confirmResolved = true;
  1224→        console.log('[Think] Sending Enter to confirm selection');
```

🤖 CLAUDE:
Toggle-thinking начинает с Escape. Если DZ активен, Escape может сбить warning. Можно сделать аналогично — DZ активен → просто подождать. Тут Escape не опасен (не `\x03`), так что await нормально. Но для toggle-thinking DZ hold = 4с — это долго. Можно тоже просто подождать.

На самом деле, toggle-thinking — менее критичный кейс. Оставлю await для него.


**Без ожидания**. Команда отправляется сразу, без `\x03`, напрямую — потому что input уже очищен первым Ctrl+C.

Перезапусти `npm run dev` и проверь — теперь переключение модели после Ctrl+C должно работать мгновенно, без 4-секундной задержки.
